Prompt: When would Karlovy Vary reach 250k residents at current rate?
Result: The population of Karlovarský kraj would take approximately **23.25 periods** to decrease to 250,000 residents at the current rate of decline (1859 residents per period).

### Converting Periods to Years
Assuming each period corresponds to 3 quarters (9 months or 0.75 years), the time required is:

\[ \text{Years Needed} = 23.25 \times 0.75 = 17.4375 \]

This is approximately **17 years and 5 months** from the current period (Q1–Q3 2024). Therefore, Karlovy Vary would reach a population of 250,000 around **Q2 2042**.

Prompt: How many women per 100 men in Olomouc at mid-year?
Result: The results are as follows:

- At mid-year, the number of men in Olomouc: **309047**
- At mid-year, the number of women in Olomouc: **322788**

To compute the number of women per 100 men:
\[
\text{Women per 100 men} = \left(\frac{\text{Number of Women}}{\text{Number of Men}}\right) \times 100
\]

\[
\text{Women per 100 men in Olomouc} = \left(\frac{322788}{309047}\right) \times 100 \approx 104.44
\]

So, there are approximately **104.44 women per 100 men in Olomouc at mid-year**.

Prompt: What if Karlovy Vary had no data for mid-period women count?
Result: To analyze and construct a pandas query based on the user prompt and schema metadata, follow these steps:

1. **Understand the User Prompt**:
   - The user is asking about a hypothetical scenario: "What if Karlovy Vary (Karlovarský kraj) had no data for mid-period women count?"
   - The query focuses on removing the data for "Karlovarský kraj" for the metric "Střední stav obyvatel - ženy" (mid-period women count).

2. **Identify Schema Mappings**:
   - **Geographical Dimension**: Match "Karlovy Vary" to its equivalent in the schema: "Karlovarský kraj."
   - **Metric Description**: Match "mid-period women count" to "Střední stav obyvatel - ženy."
   - **Value Column**: The column holding the numerical data is named `value`.

3. **Construct the Query**:
   - To simulate the absence of data for "Karlovarský kraj" and "Střední stav obyvatel - ženy," we can filter out those rows from the dataset.

### Pandas Query:
```python
df = df[~((df["ČR, kraje"] == "Karlovarský kraj") & (df["Ukazatel"] == "Střední stav obyvatel - ženy"))]
```

This query filters out rows where:
- "ČR, kraje" (Region) is "Karlovarský kraj," and
- "Ukazatel" (Metric) is "Střední stav obyvatel - ženy."

Shall I execute this query to validate and return the updated dataset?

Prompt: When would Karlovy Vary reach 250k residents at current rate?
Result: The population data for Karlovarský kraj is as follows:
- Population at the beginning of the period: 295077
- Population at the end of the period: 293218

### Step 1: Calculate the Growth Rate
The population decreased during the period, so the growth rate is negative:
\[
\text{Growth Rate} = \text{Population at End} - \text{Population at Start}
\]
\[
\text{Growth Rate} = 293218 - 295077 = -1859
\]

### Step 2: Project Timeline for 250,000 Residents
Given the current negative growth rate of -1859 per period, Karlovarský kraj is moving away from the target population of 250,000. The population is declining, so it would not reach 250,000 residents under the current trend.

### Conclusion
At the current rate of population decline (-1859 per period), Karlovarský kraj is not on track to reach 250,000 residents. Instead, its population is decreasing further from this target.

import pandas as pd

- **Men**: 301,029

### Bar Chart:

Below is a bar chart representation of the data:

```python
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Data
categories = ['Men', 'Women']
prague_values = [670680, 714052]
plzen_values = [301029, 312345]

# Bar chart
x = range(len(categories))
plt.bar(x, prague_values, width=0.4, label='Prague', align='center', color='blue')
plt.bar([p + 0.4 for p in x], plzen_values, width=0.4, label='Plzeň', align='center', color='orange')

# Labels and title
plt.xticks([p + 0.2 for p in x], categories)
plt.ylabel('Population')
plt.title('Comparison of Men and Women in Prague and Plzeň')
plt.legend()

# Show plot
plt.show()
```

This chart will visually compare the number of men and women in Prague and Plzeň, clearly showing the differences in population.

Prompt: Find records where male count equals female count
Result: The question asks to find records where the male count equals the female count in the dataset. However, all three queries executed to achieve this goal resulted in errors. Below is an analysis of each query and the issues encountered:

---

### **Query 1 Analysis**
- **Query:** The query attempts to filter rows where the indicator (`Ukazatel`) is "Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži" and the `value` column matches the `value` column for rows where the indicator is "Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy".
- **Error:** `Can only compare identically-labeled Series objects`.
- **Reason:** The comparison is being made between two Series objects that do not have identical indices. Without aligning the indices, the comparison cannot proceed.

---

### **Query 2 Analysis**
- **Query:** This query improves upon the first by setting the index for the female population data (`Ukazatel == 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy'`) to `['Kumulace čtvrtletí', 'ČR, kraje']`. The intention is to align the data for comparison.
- **Error:** `Can only compare identically-labeled Series objects`.
- **Reason:** Although the index for the female population data is set, the male population data is not similarly indexed. As a result, the two Series objects still do not have identical indices, leading to the same error as in Query 1.

---

### **Query 3 Analysis**
- **Query:** This query further refines the approach by reindexing the female population data to match the index of the male population data. The goal is to ensure that both Series objects have identical indices before comparison.
- **Error:** `('Lengths must match to compare', (135,), (15,))`.
- **Reason:** The male population data contains 135 rows, while the female population data contains only 15 rows. Reindexing does not resolve the mismatch in lengths, and the comparison fails because the two Series objects must have the same length to be compared element-wise.

---

### **Conclusion**
The errors indicate that the dataset is not structured in a way that allows for direct comparison between male and female population counts. Specifically:
1. The male and female population data have different numbers of rows (135 vs. 15).
2. The indices of the two datasets are not aligned, making element-wise comparison impossible.

To resolve this issue:
- Ensure that both male and female population data are filtered to the same set of indices (e.g., by using a common key such as `['Kumulace čtvrtletí', 'ČR, kraje']`).
- Verify that the lengths of the two datasets match after filtering.
- Perform the comparison only after these steps.

Without restructuring the data or additional information about its organization, it is not possible to identify records where the male count equals the female count.

Result: ### Analysis:

The query results provide the population data for men and women in two regions: **Hlavní město Praha (Prague)** and **Plzeňský kraj (Plzeň)**. Below is the comparison:

#### Population in Prague:
- **Men**: 670,680
- **Women**: 714,052
- **Difference**: There are 43,372 more women than men in Prague.

#### Population in Plzeň:
- **Men**: 301,029
- **Women**: 312,345
- **Difference**: There are 11,316 more women than men in Plzeň.

#### Comparison Between Regions:
- Prague has a significantly larger population than Plzeň for both men and women.
  - **Men**: Prague has 369,651 more men than Plzeň (670,680 vs. 301,029).
  - **Women**: Prague has 401,707 more women than Plzeň (714,052 vs. 312,345).
- The gender imbalance (more women than men) is present in both regions, but the absolute difference is larger in Prague (43,372) compared to Plzeň (11,316).

### Bar Chart:

Below is a bar chart representation of the data:

```python
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Data
regions = ['Prague', 'Plzeň']
men = [670680, 301029]
women = [714052, 312345]

# Bar chart
x = range(len(regions))
plt.bar(x, men, width=0.4, label='Men', color='blue', align='center')
plt.bar(x, women, width=0.4, label='Women', color='pink', align='edge')

# Labels and title
plt.xticks(x, regions)
plt.ylabel('Population')
plt.title('Population of Men and Women in Prague and Plzeň')
plt.legend()

# Show plot
plt.show()
```

This chart visually compares the number of men and women in both regions, highlighting the differences in population size and gender distribution.

Prompt: How much did Prague's population grow from start to end of Q3?
Result: The original question asks about the population growth in Prague from the start to the end of Q3 2024. However, the queries executed to retrieve this information encountered issues due to incorrect table references.

### Analysis of Query Results:
1. **Query 1** attempted to calculate the population growth directly by subtracting the population at the start of the period from the population at the end of the period. However, it failed with the error: `no such table: Počet obyvatel`. This indicates that the table name "Počet obyvatel" does not exist in the database.

2. **Query 2** aimed to retrieve the population at the start of the period (Q1-Q3 2024) but also failed with the same error: `no such table: Počet obyvatel`.

3. **Query 3** listed the available tables in the database. The result shows two tables: `OBY01PDT01` and `OBY01PDT01____2`. This confirms that the table "Počet obyvatel" does not exist, and the queries should have targeted one of these available tables instead.

### Conclusion:
The queries failed to retrieve the required data due to incorrect table references. To answer the original question, the correct table (likely `OBY01PDT01` or `OBY01PDT01____2`) must be identified and queried for the relevant population data. Prompt: How many women per 100 men in Olomouc at mid-year?
Result: Based on the query results, we can determine the number of women per 100 men in Olomouc at mid-year (Q1-Q3 2024) as follows:

1. **Women per 100 men**:
   - Query 1 directly calculates the ratio of women to men, multiplied by 100, resulting in **104.44624927600009 women per 100 men**.

2. **Total population breakdown**:
   - Query 2 provides the total number of women and men:
     - Total women: **322,788**
     - Total men: **309,047**
   - Using these totals, we can independently verify the ratio:
     \[
     \text{Women per 100 men} = \left(\frac{\text{Total women}}{\text{Total men}}\right) \times 100 = \left(\frac{322,788}{309,047}\right) \times 100 = 104.44624927600009
     \]
   - This matches the result from Query 1.

3. **Individual data points**:
   - Query 3 confirms the same values for the mid-year population:
     - Men: **309,047**
     - Women: **322,788**

### Conclusion:
In Olomouc (Olomoucký kraj) at mid-year (Q1-Q3 2024), there are **104.44624927600009 women per 100 men**. This means there are approximately 4.45% more women than men in the region.

  Result: 104.44624927600009
  Query: SELECT SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS total_women, SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS total_men FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Olomoucký kraj' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
  Result: [(322788, 309047)]
  Query: SELECT "Ukazatel", value FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Olomoucký kraj' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "Ukazatel" IN ('Střední stav obyvatel - ženy', 'Střední stav obyvatel - muži') LIMIT 5

3. **Jihomoravský kraj** (South Moravian Region) has a much smaller growth rate of **0.0006146326591666266** (approximately 0.06%). While positive, the growth here is significantly lower compared to the top two regions.

4. **Česko** (Czech Republic as a whole) shows a slight population decline with a growth rate of **-0.0003043881710610148** (approximately -0.03%). This suggests that, overall, the country's population decreased slightly during the period analyzed.

5. **Plzeňský kraj** (Plzeň Region) has the lowest growth rate in this ranking, at **-0.00043203657148819483** (approximately -0.04%). This indicates a small population decline in this region.

- The regions with negative growth rates are **Česko** (overall) and **Plzeňský kraj**, with Plzeň experiencing the largest relative decline among the listed regions.

Prompt: Can you compare number of man and number of woman in prague and in plzen? Create me a bar chart with this data.
Result: ### Analysis of the Population Data for Prague and Plzeň

The query results provide the number of men and women in two regions of the Czech Republic: **Hlavní město Praha (Prague)** and **Plzeňský kraj (Plzeň Region)**. Below is the detailed comparison:

#### Population in Prague:
- **Men**: 670,680
- **Women**: 714,052
- **Difference**: There are 43,372 more women than men in Prague.

#### Population in Plzeň:
- **Men**: 301,029
- **Women**: 312,345
- **Difference**: There are 11,316 more women than men in Plzeň.

#### Comparison Between Prague and Plzeň:
- Prague has a significantly larger population than Plzeň for both men and women.
  - **Men**: Prague has 369,651 more men than Plzeň (670,680 vs. 301,029).
  - **Women**: Prague has 401,707 more women than Plzeň (714,052 vs. 312,345).
- The gender imbalance (more women than men) is present in both regions, but the absolute difference is larger in Prague (43,372) compared to Plzeň (11,316).

### Bar Chart Representation

Below is a bar chart to visualize the data:

```python
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Data
regions = ['Prague', 'Plzeň']
men = [670680, 301029]
women = [714052, 312345]

# Bar chart
x = range(len(regions))
plt.bar(x, men, width=0.4, label='Men', color='blue', align='center')
plt.bar(x, women, width=0.4, label='Women', color='pink', align='edge')

# Labels and title
plt.xlabel('Regions')
plt.ylabel('Population')
plt.title('Comparison of Men and Women in Prague and Plzeň')
plt.xticks(x, regions)
plt.legend()

# Show plot
plt.show()
```

This chart will clearly display the population of men and women in both regions, highlighting the differences.

Prompt: What was South Bohemia's population change rate per month?
Result: The question asks for the population change rate per month in South Bohemia (Jihočeský kraj) for the period Q1-Q3 2024.

### Analysis:

1. **Monthly Change Rate Calculation**:
   - From **Query 1**, the result for the monthly change rate is `0.0`. This suggests that the calculation `(MAX(value) - MIN(value)) / 9.0` yielded zero, indicating no significant change in population over the 9 months of Q1-Q3 2024.

2. **Population Data**:
   - From **Query 2**, the population at the beginning of the period (Q1-Q3 2024) was **654,505**, and at the end of the period, it was **653,346**.
   - The total population change over the 9 months is:
     \[
     653,346 - 654,505 = -1,159
     \]
   - The monthly change rate can be calculated as:
     \[
     \text{Monthly Change Rate} = \frac{-1,159}{9} = -128.7777 \text{ (approximately -128.78 people per month)}.
     \]

3. **Discrepancy**:
   - The result from **Query 1** (0.0) does not align with the actual population data from **Query 2**, which shows a decline of 1,159 people over the period. This discrepancy suggests that the calculation in **Query 1** may have been affected by rounding or data processing issues.

### Conclusion:
The population of South Bohemia (Jihočeský kraj) decreased by **1,159 people** over the 9 months of Q1-Q3 2024, resulting in an average monthly change rate of approximately **-128.78 people per month**. However, the query calculation in **Query 1** returned a rate of `0.0`, which appears to be incorrect based on the provided data.

Prompt: Rank regions by population growth rate from start to end
Result: The query results provide the population growth rates for various regions in the Czech Republic, ranked from highest to lowest. Below is the analysis:

1. **Hlavní město Praha** has the highest population growth rate at **0.0053389392315624975** (approximately 0.53%). This indicates that Prague experienced the most significant relative population increase among the regions analyzed.

2. **Středočeský kraj** follows with a growth rate of **0.004582606426088987** (approximately 0.46%). This region also saw a notable population increase, though slightly less than Prague.

3. **Jihomoravský kraj** is third with a growth rate of **0.0006146326591666266** (approximately 0.06%). While positive, the growth here is much smaller compared to the top two regions.

4. **Česko** (the entire Czech Republic) has a slight population decline, with a growth rate of **-0.0003043881710610148** (approximately -0.03%). This indicates that, overall, the country's population decreased slightly during the period analyzed.

5. **Plzeňský kraj** has the lowest growth rate in this ranking, at **-0.00043203657148819483** (approximately -0.04%). This region experienced a small population decline.

### Summary:
- The regions with positive growth rates are **Hlavní město Praha**, **Středočeský kraj**, and **Jihomoravský kraj**.
- The regions with negative growth rates are **Česko** (overall) and **Plzeňský kraj**.
- **Hlavní město Praha** leads in population growth, while **Plzeňský kraj** shows the most significant decline among the listed regions.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", (SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) * 1.0 / SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS growth_rate FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem') GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ORDER BY growth_rate DESC LIMIT 5
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha', 0.0053389392315624975), ('Středočeský kraj', 0.004582606426088987), ('Jihomoravský kraj', 0.0006146326591666266), ('Česko', -0.0003043881710610148), ('Plzeňský kraj', -0.00043203657148819483)]

Prompt: What if Karlovy Vary had no data for mid-period women count?
Result: The question asks about the implications if Karlovy Vary (Karlovarský kraj) had no data for the mid-period women count ("Střední stav obyvatel - ženy") for Q1-Q3 2024. Let us analyze the provided data:

### Data Summary:
1. **Mid-period women count ("Střední stav obyvatel - ženy")**:
   - Value: **150,583** (from Query 1).

2. **Mid-period total population ("Střední stav obyvatel - celkem")**:
   - Value: **293,714** (from Query 2).

3. **Mid-period men count ("Střední stav obyvatel - muži")**:
   - Value: **143,131** (from Query 3).

### Analysis:
If the data for women were missing, we could estimate it using the total population and the men count. The formula would be:

\[
\text{Women count} = \text{Total population} - \text{Men count}
\]

Substituting the known values:
\[
\text{Women count} = 293,714 - 143,131 = 150,583
\]

This calculated value matches the provided value for women (150,583). Therefore, even if the women count data were missing, it could be accurately derived from the total population and men count.

### Conclusion:
If Karlovy Vary had no data for the mid-period women count, it would not pose a significant issue because the women count can be precisely calculated using the total population and men count. The consistency of the data ensures that the derived value (150,583) aligns with the recorded value.

  Result: [('Karlovarský kraj', 'Střední stav obyvatel - ženy', 150583)]
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", "Ukazatel", "value" FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Karlovarský kraj' AND "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - celkem' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' LIMIT 5

Prompt: Rank regions by population growth rate from start to end
Result: The query results provide the population growth rates for various regions in the Czech Republic, ranked in descending order. Here is the analysis:

1. **Hlavní město Praha** has the highest population growth rate at **0.0053389392315624975** (approximately 0.53%). This indicates that Prague experienced the most significant relative population increase among the regions analyzed.

2. **Středočeský kraj** follows with a growth rate of **0.004582606426088987** (approximately 0.46%). This region also saw a notable population increase, though slightly less than Prague.

3. **Jihomoravský kraj** ranks third with a much smaller growth rate of **0.0006146326591666266** (approximately 0.06%). While positive, the growth here is significantly lower compared to the top two regions.

4. **Česko** (the entire Czech Republic) shows a slight population decline with a growth rate of **-0.0003043881710610148** (approximately -0.03%). This suggests that, overall, the country experienced a small population decrease during the period analyzed.

5. **Plzeňský kraj** has the lowest growth rate in this ranking, at **-0.00043203657148819483** (approximately -0.04%). This indicates a marginal population decline in this region.

### Summary:
- The regions with positive growth rates are **Hlavní město Praha**, **Středočeský kraj**, and **Jihomoravský kraj**.
- The regions with negative growth rates are **Česko** (overall) and **Plzeňský kraj**.
- **Hlavní město Praha** and **Středočeský kraj** stand out as the only regions with relatively significant population growth, while the other regions show minimal or negative changes.

  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", ((SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END)) * 1.0 / SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END)) AS growth_rate FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem') GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ORDER BY growth_rate DESC LIMIT 5

However, the result of the query indicates that **no such regions exist** in the dataset.

### Analysis:
1. **Condition 1**: The mid-period population must be less than the start-of-period population.
2. **Condition 2**: The mid-period population must be greater than the end-of-period population.
3. The query checks for regions that satisfy both conditions simultaneously.

Since no results were returned, it can be concluded that **no region in the dataset meets these criteria**. In other words, for all regions, the mid-period population does not fall strictly between the start-of-period and end-of-period populations in the specified manner.

Prompt: tell me about people in prague, compare, contrast, what is interesting, provide trends.
Result: Na základě poskytnutých výsledků dotazů lze analyzovat demografické údaje o obyvatelích Prahy a porovnat je s jinými kraji v České republice. Zde je kompletní analýza:

### 1. **Počet obyvatel v Praze**
- Na počátku období Q1-Q3 2024 měla Praha celkem **1 384 732 obyvatel**, z toho **670 680 mužů** a **714 052 žen**.
- Na konci stejného období vzrostl počet obyvatel na **1 392 125**, což představuje nárůst o **7 393 obyvatel**. Tento růst byl rovnoměrně rozdělen mezi muže (**676 069**) a ženy (**716 056**).

### 2. **Střední stav obyvatel**
- Střední stav obyvatel v Praze (průměrný počet obyvatel během období) byl **1 386 723**, z toho **672 752 mužů** a **713 971 žen**.
- Praha má tedy mírně vyšší podíl žen než mužů, což je trend, který se odráží i v dalších ukazatelích.

### 3. **Porovnání s jinými kraji**
- **Jihočeský kraj**:
  - Střední stav obyvatel byl **653 412**, což je méně než polovina středního stavu obyvatel Prahy.
  - Počet mužů v Jihočeském kraji byl **322 004**, což je méně než polovina mužů v Praze (**672 752**).
- Praha má tedy výrazně vyšší počet obyvatel než Jihočeský kraj, což odpovídá jejímu postavení hlavního města a centra ekonomické aktivity.

### 4. **Trendy a zajímavosti**
- **Růst populace v Praze**: Během období Q1-Q3 2024 došlo k nárůstu počtu obyvatel o **7 393 osob**, což naznačuje pokračující trend růstu populace v hlavním městě.
- **Vyšší podíl žen**: Ve všech ukazatelích (počet obyvatel na počátku a konci období, střední stav obyvatel) je patrný vyšší podíl žen oproti mužům. Tento trend může být způsoben delší střední délkou života žen nebo jinými demografickými faktory.
- **Významné rozdíly oproti menším krajům**: Praha má více než dvojnásobný počet obyvatel oproti Jihočeskému kraji, což zdůrazňuje její roli jako nejlidnatějšího regionu v ČR.

### 5. **Závěr**
Praha je demograficky nejvýznamnějším regionem v České republice s rostoucí populací a vyšším podílem žen. Ve srovnání s menšími kraji, jako je Jihočeský kraj, má Praha výrazně vyšší počet obyvatel, což odpovídá jejímu postavení hlavního města. Trend růstu populace naznačuje, že Praha zůstává atraktivním místem pro život a práci.

### Počet obyvatel a struktura
1. **Celkový počet obyvatel**:
   - Na počátku období Q1-Q3 2024 činil počet obyvatel Prahy 1,384,732, zatímco střední stav obyvatel byl o něco vyšší, a to 1,386,723. Na konci období se počet obyvatel zvýšil na 1,392,125, což naznačuje mírný růst populace během sledovaného období.

2. **Rozdělení podle pohlaví**:
   - Na počátku období bylo v Praze 670,680 mužů a 714,052 žen, což ukazuje, že ženy tvoří větší část populace (přibližně 51.6 % žen oproti 48.4 % mužů). Tento trend je potvrzen i na konci období, kdy počet žen dosáhl 716,056.

### Srovnání s ostatními regiony a celou ČR
1. **Celkový počet obyvatel**:
   - Praha je druhým nejlidnatějším regionem v ČR po Středočeském kraji, který měl střední stav obyvatel 1,458,238 a počet obyvatel na počátku období 1,455,940. Celkově má Česká republika na počátku období 10,900,555 obyvatel, což znamená, že Praha představuje přibližně 12.7 % celkové populace ČR.

2. **Rozdělení podle pohlaví v ČR**:
   - V celé ČR bylo na počátku období 5,557,945 žen a 5,342,610 mužů, což potvrzuje obecný trend, že ženy tvoří větší část populace. Tento trend je patrný i v Praze, kde ženy tvoří větší podíl než muži.

### Zajímavé trendy
1. **Růst populace v Praze**:
   - Během sledovaného období (Q1-Q3 2024) došlo k nárůstu počtu obyvatel v Praze o 7,393 osob (z 1,384,732 na 1,392,125). Tento růst může být způsoben přirozeným přírůstkem, migrací nebo jinými faktory.

2. **Vyšší podíl žen**:
   - V Praze je podíl žen vyšší než mužů, což odpovídá celorepublikovému trendu. Tento rozdíl je však v Praze výraznější než v některých jiných regionech, například ve Středočeském kraji.

3. **Stabilní střední stav obyvatel**:
   - Střední stav obyvatel v Praze (1,386,723) je velmi blízký počtu obyvatel na počátku období (1,384,732), což naznačuje relativní stabilitu populace během sledovaného období.

Prompt: List regions where women population decreased >1000
Result: Regions where the women population decreased by more than 1000 are:

1. Moravskoslezský kraj (3299)
2. Ústecký kraj (1466)
3. Karlovarský kraj (1228)
4. Liberecký kraj (1142)
5. Plzeňský kraj (1073)
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS decrease
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy')
  AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
HAVING decrease > 1000
LIMIT 5;
  Result: [('Karlovarský kraj', 1228), ('Liberecký kraj', 1142), ('Moravskoslezský kraj', 3299), ('Plzeňský kraj', 1073), ('Ústecký kraj', 1466)]
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS decrease
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy')
  AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"

Prompt: List regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes was greater than 1000, and indicate whether men or women changed more
Result: Regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes was greater than 1000 are:

1. **Hlavní město Praha**: Men changed more (male change: 5389, female change: 2004, absolute difference: 3385).
2. **Jihomoravský kraj**: Men changed more (male change: 1059, female change: -305, absolute difference: 1364).
3. **Plzeňský kraj**: Men changed more (male change: 808, female change: -1073, absolute difference: 1881).
4. **Středočeský kraj**: Men changed more (male change: 4252, female change: 2420, absolute difference: 1832).

Contradiction: In Result 1, "Hlavní město Praha" and "Jihomoravský kraj" are listed as regions where women changed more, but Result 2 shows men changed more in these regions.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
       CASE WHEN ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) > 1000 
            THEN CASE WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) > SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) 
                      THEN 'Men' ELSE 'Women' END 
            ELSE NULL END AS "Dominant Gender"
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
HAVING ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) > 1000
LIMIT 5;
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha', 'Women'), ('Jihomoravský kraj', 'Women'), ('Jihočeský kraj', 'Women'), ('Karlovarský kraj', 'Women'), ('Kraj Vysočina', 'Women')]
  Query: WITH male_changes AS (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) -
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS male_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
female_changes AS (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) -
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS female_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT m.region, 
       ABS(m.male_change - f.female_change) AS abs_difference,
       CASE WHEN m.male_change > f.female_change THEN 'Men' ELSE 'Women' END AS greater_change,
       m.male_change, 
       f.female_change
FROM male_changes m
JOIN female_changes f ON m.region = f.region
WHERE ABS(m.male_change - f.female_change) > 1000;
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha', 3385, 'Men', 5389, 2004), ('Jihomoravský kraj', 1364, 'Men', 1059, -305), ('Plzeňský kraj', 1881, 'Men', 808, -1073), ('Středočeský kraj', 1832, 'Men', 4252, 2420)]

            THEN CASE WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) > SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) 
                      THEN 'Men' ELSE 'Women' END 
            ELSE NULL END AS "Dominant Gender"
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
HAVING ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) > 1000
LIMIT 5;
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha', 'Women'), ('Jihomoravský kraj', 'Women'), ('Jihočeský kraj', 'Women'), ('Karlovarský kraj', 'Women'), ('Kraj Vysočina', 'Women')]

         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS male_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'

  AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'

LIMIT 5;

  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        (CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - 
        (CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS population_change
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem')
),
MeanVariance AS (
    SELECT 
        region,
        AVG(population_change) AS mean_change,
        AVG((population_change - AVG(population_change)) * (population_change - AVG(population_change))) AS variance
    FROM PopulationChange
    WHERE region != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY region
)
SELECT 
    region,
    MAX(SQRT(variance)) AS max_stddev
FROM MeanVariance
LIMIT 5;

  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS ( 
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) -
        MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS population_change
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem')
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje", "Kumulace čtvrtletí"
),
MeanChange AS (
    SELECT 
        region,
        AVG(population_change) AS mean_change
    FROM PopulationChange
    WHERE region != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY region
)
SELECT 
    pc.region,
    SQRT(AVG((pc.population_change - mc.mean_change) * (pc.population_change - mc.mean_change))) AS stddev
FROM PopulationChange pc
JOIN MeanChange mc ON pc.region = mc.region
GROUP BY pc.region
ORDER BY stddev DESC
LIMIT 5;

Prompt: List regions where both male and female populations increased, but the increase was not proportional (difference in growth rates > 0.5%)
Result: The only region where both male and female populations increased, but the increase was not proportional (difference in growth rates > 0.5%), is **Hlavní město Praha**. The male growth rate is 0.008035128526271843, while the female growth rate is 0.0028065182927853993.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH male_growth AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value END) - 
     MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END)) * 1.0 / 
     MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_male
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),

female_growth AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value END) - 
     MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END)) * 1.0 / 
     MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_female
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)

SELECT 
  m.region,
  m.growth_rate_male,
  f.growth_rate_female
FROM male_growth m
JOIN female_growth f ON m.region = f.region
WHERE ABS(m.growth_rate_male - f.growth_rate_female) > 0.005
LIMIT 5;
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha', 0.008035128526271843, 0.0028065182927853993), ('Plzeňský kraj', 0.0026841267784831362, -0.003435303910739727)]
  Query: WITH male_growth AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value END) - MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END)) * 1.0 / MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_male FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ), female_growth AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value END) - MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END)) * 1.0 / MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_female FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ) SELECT m.region, m.growth_rate_male, f.growth_rate_female FROM male_growth m JOIN female_growth f ON m.region = f.region WHERE m.growth_rate_male > 0 AND f.growth_rate_female > 0 AND ABS(m.growth_rate_male - f.growth_rate_female) > 0.005;

  Query: WITH gender_ratios AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS gender_ratio
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Střední stav obyvatel - ženy', 'Střední stav obyvatel - muži')
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)

FROM gender_ratios;

Prompt: Which regions had a higher percentage of women at the end of the period compared to the start, despite having a net population decrease?
Result: Ústecký kraj had a higher percentage of women at the end of the period (0.5076335641735348) compared to the start (0.5075871982287291), despite experiencing a net population decrease of -2962.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_female_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_female_population
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT 
    region,
    (end_female_population * 1.0 / NULLIF(end_population, 0)) AS end_female_percentage,
    (start_female_population * 1.0 / NULLIF(start_population, 0)) AS start_female_percentage,
    (end_population - start_population) AS net_population_change
FROM PopulationChange
WHERE 
    (end_female_population * 1.0 / NULLIF(end_population, 0)) > (start_female_population * 1.0 / NULLIF(start_population, 0))
    AND (end_population - start_population) < 0
LIMIT 5;

  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_female_percentage,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_female_percentage,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS net_population_decrease
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT region
FROM FemalePercentage
WHERE end_female_percentage > start_female_percentage
  AND net_population_decrease > 0;

    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
NationalPopulation AS (
  SELECT 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS national_start_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko'
)

  region,

Prompt: What was the average population change rate per month for regions that lost population, weighted by their initial population?
Result: The average population change rate per month for regions that lost population, weighted by their initial population, was -0.00013442712843835756.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS initial_population,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) AS final_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING final_population < initial_population
), WeightedChangeRate AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    (final_population - initial_population) * 1.0 / initial_population / 9 AS monthly_change_rate, -- 9 months in Q1-Q3
    initial_population
  FROM PopulationChange
)
SELECT 
  SUM(monthly_change_rate * initial_population) / SUM(initial_population) AS weighted_avg_monthly_change_rate
FROM WeightedChangeRate;
  Result: -0.00013442712843835756
  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS initial_population,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) AS final_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING final_population < initial_population
), WeightedChangeRate AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    (final_population - initial_population) * 1.0 / initial_population / 9 AS monthly_change_rate, -- 9 months in Q1-Q3
    initial_population
  FROM PopulationChange
)
SELECT 
  SUM(monthly_change_rate * initial_population) / SUM(initial_population) AS weighted_avg_monthly_change_rate
FROM WeightedChangeRate;
  Result: -0.00013442712843835756

Prompt: What was the weighted average population change rate, where weights are based on the region's share of total national population?
Result: The weighted average population change rate, where weights are based on the region's share of the total national population, is -0.00030438817106101464.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH PopulationData AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_population,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
NationalPopulation AS (
  SELECT 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS total_start_population,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS total_end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko'
),
WeightedChange AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    (end_population - start_population) * 1.0 / start_population AS change_rate,
    start_population * 1.0 / (SELECT total_start_population FROM NationalPopulation) AS weight
  FROM PopulationData
)
SELECT 
  SUM(change_rate * weight) AS weighted_average_change_rate
FROM WeightedChange;

Prompt: Which region had the most stable gender ratio throughout the period (smallest standard deviation of gender ratio across start, middle, and end)?
Result: The region with the most stable gender ratio throughout the period is **Ústecký kraj**, with the smallest variance of **3.1907030547173734e-08**.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT "ČR, kraje", STDDEV(gender_ratio) AS stddev_gender_ratio
FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         (SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
          SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) AS gender_ratio
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" IN (
    'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži',
    'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy',
    'Střední stav obyvatel - muži',
    'Střední stav obyvatel - ženy',
    'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži',
    'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy'
  )
  AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje", "Ukazatel"
) subquery
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
ORDER BY stddev_gender_ratio ASC
LIMIT 5;
  Result: Error: Query error: no such function: STDDEV
  Query: WITH GenderRatios AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN 'male'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN 'female'
    END AS gender,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%počátku%' THEN 'start'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%Střední%' THEN 'middle'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%konci%' THEN 'end'
    END AS period,
    SUM(value) AS total
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' OR "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%'
  GROUP BY region, gender, period
),
GenderRatiosPivot AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'male' THEN total END) AS male_total,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'female' THEN total END) AS female_total
  FROM GenderRatios
  GROUP BY region, period
),
GenderRatioStats AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    AVG(CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total) AS mean_ratio,
    SUM(POWER((CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total) - AVG(CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total), 2)) / COUNT(*) AS variance
  FROM GenderRatiosPivot
  GROUP BY region
)
SELECT 
  region,
  MIN(SQRT(variance)) AS smallest_std_dev
FROM GenderRatioStats
WHERE region != 'Česko'
GROUP BY region
ORDER BY smallest_std_dev ASC
LIMIT 5;
  Result: Error: Query error: no such function: POWER
  Query: WITH GenderRatios AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN 'male'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN 'female'
    END AS gender,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%počátku%' THEN 'start'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%Střední%' THEN 'middle'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%konci%' THEN 'end'
    END AS period,
    SUM(value) AS total
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' OR "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%'
  GROUP BY region, gender, period
),
GenderRatiosPivot AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'male' THEN total END) AS male_total,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'female' THEN total END) AS female_total
  FROM GenderRatios
  GROUP BY region, period
),
GenderRatioCalc AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    male_total * 1.0 / female_total AS gender_ratio
  FROM GenderRatiosPivot
),
MeanGenderRatio AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    AVG(gender_ratio) AS mean_ratio
  FROM GenderRatioCalc
  GROUP BY region
),
VarianceCalc AS (
  SELECT 
    g.region,
    AVG((g.gender_ratio - m.mean_ratio) * (g.gender_ratio - m.mean_ratio)) AS variance
  FROM GenderRatioCalc g
  JOIN MeanGenderRatio m ON g.region = m.region
  GROUP BY g.region
)
SELECT 
  region,
  MIN(variance) AS min_variance
FROM VarianceCalc
WHERE region != 'Česko'
LIMIT 5;

         (SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
          SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) AS gender_ratio
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" IN (
    'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži',
    'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy',
    'Střední stav obyvatel - muži',
    'Střední stav obyvatel - ženy',
    'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži',
    'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy'
  )
  AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje", "Ukazatel"
) subquery
GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
ORDER BY stddev_gender_ratio ASC
LIMIT 5;

  Query: WITH GenderRatios AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN 'male'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN 'female'
    END AS gender,
    CASE 
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%počátku%' THEN 'start'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%Střední%' THEN 'middle'
      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%konci%' THEN 'end'
    END AS period,
    SUM(value) AS total
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' OR "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%'
  GROUP BY region, gender, period
),
GenderRatiosPivot AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'male' THEN total END) AS male_total,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'female' THEN total END) AS female_total
  FROM GenderRatios
  GROUP BY region, period
),
GenderRatioStats AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    AVG(CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total) AS mean_ratio,
    SUM(POWER((CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total) - AVG(CAST(male_total AS FLOAT) / female_total), 2)) / COUNT(*) AS variance
  FROM GenderRatiosPivot
  GROUP BY region
)
SELECT 
  region,
  MIN(SQRT(variance)) AS smallest_std_dev
FROM GenderRatioStats
WHERE region != 'Česko'
GROUP BY region
ORDER BY smallest_std_dev ASC
LIMIT 5;

      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN 'female'

      WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%Střední%' THEN 'middle'

  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'male' THEN total END) AS male_total,
    MAX(CASE WHEN gender = 'female' THEN total END) AS female_total
  FROM GenderRatios
  GROUP BY region, period
),
GenderRatioCalc AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    period,
    male_total * 1.0 / female_total AS gender_ratio
  FROM GenderRatiosPivot
),
MeanGenderRatio AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    AVG(gender_ratio) AS mean_ratio
  FROM GenderRatioCalc
  GROUP BY region

Prompt: Which regions had a population change pattern that was opposite to the national trend (increased when national decreased or vice versa)?
Result: The regions with a population change pattern opposite to the national trend are:

- **Hlavní město Praha**: Regional trend is "Increase" while national trend is "Decrease".
- **Jihomoravský kraj**: Regional trend is "Increase" while national trend is "Decrease".
- **Středočeský kraj**: Regional trend is "Increase" while national trend is "Decrease".
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH NationalTrend AS (
    SELECT 
        CASE 
            WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - 
                 SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) > 0 THEN 'Increase'
            ELSE 'Decrease'
        END AS trend
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
),
RegionalTrends AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        CASE 
            WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - 
                 SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) > 0 THEN 'Increase'
            ELSE 'Decrease'
        END AS trend
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT region
FROM RegionalTrends, NationalTrend
WHERE RegionalTrends.trend != NationalTrend.trend
LIMIT 5;
  Result: [('Hlavní město Praha',), ('Jihomoravský kraj',), ('Středočeský kraj',)]
  Query: WITH NationalTrend AS ( SELECT CASE WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) > 0 THEN 'Increase' ELSE 'Decrease' END AS trend FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' ), RegionalTrends AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, CASE WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) - SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) > 0 THEN 'Increase' ELSE 'Decrease' END AS trend FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ) SELECT RegionalTrends.region, RegionalTrends.trend AS regional_trend, NationalTrend.trend AS national_trend FROM RegionalTrends, NationalTrend WHERE RegionalTrends.trend != NationalTrend.trend;

Result: The question cannot be answered because all attempts to calculate the standard deviation and identify regions with gender ratios more than 2 standard deviations away from the mean failed due to missing functions (`STDDEV`, `POWER`, `SQRT`).
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH GenderRatios AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value END) AS male_population,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value END) AS female_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
GenderRatiosWithStats AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    male_population,
    female_population,
    CAST(male_population AS FLOAT) / female_population AS gender_ratio,
    AVG(CAST(male_population AS FLOAT) / female_population) OVER () AS mean_ratio,
    STDDEV(CAST(male_population AS FLOAT) / female_population) OVER () AS stddev_ratio
  FROM GenderRatios
)
SELECT 
  region,
  gender_ratio,
  mean_ratio,
  stddev_ratio
FROM GenderRatiosWithStats
WHERE ABS(gender_ratio - mean_ratio) > 2 * stddev_ratio
LIMIT 5;

            THEN CASE WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) > SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) 
                      THEN 'Men' ELSE 'Women' END

Prompt: How many regions had a higher percentage of women at period end despite population decrease?
Result: 11 regions had a higher percentage of women at period end despite a population decrease.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_female_population
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
FilteredRegions AS (
    SELECT 
        region,
        end_female_population * 100.0 / NULLIF(end_population, 0) AS female_percentage_end,
        start_population,
        end_population
    FROM PopulationChange
    WHERE end_population < start_population
)
SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_higher_female_percentage
FROM FilteredRegions
WHERE female_percentage_end > 50;
  Result: 11
  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_female_population
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
FilteredRegions AS (
    SELECT 
        region,
        end_female_population * 100.0 / NULLIF(end_population, 0) AS female_percentage_end,
        start_population,
        end_population
    FROM PopulationChange
    WHERE end_population < start_population
)

FROM FilteredRegions

    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
        "Kumulace čtvrtletí" AS period, 
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) * 1.0 / 
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS gender_ratio
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži', 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy')
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY region, period
),
MeanRatios AS (
    SELECT 
        region, 
        AVG(gender_ratio) AS mean_ratio
    FROM GenderRatios
    GROUP BY region
),
VarianceCalc AS (
    SELECT 
        g.region, 
        AVG((g.gender_ratio - m.mean_ratio) * (g.gender_ratio - m.mean_ratio)) AS variance
    FROM GenderRatios g
    JOIN MeanRatios m ON g.region = m.region
    GROUP BY g.region
)
SELECT 
    region, 
    MIN(variance) AS min_variance
FROM VarianceCalc
LIMIT 1;

Result: The median population size of regions that experienced a population increase is 6672.0.

  Query: WITH PopulationChange AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) -
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS population_change
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
    HAVING region != 'Česko' AND population_change > 0

    FROM PopulationChange
)

    AVG(population_change) AS median_population_change
FROM RankedRegions
WHERE row_num IN ((total_rows + 1) / 2, (total_rows + 2) / 2);

Prompt: What is the total number of regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes exceeded 1000?
Result: The total number of regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes exceeded 1000 is 14.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT "ČR, kraje") AS region_count
FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
             SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) AS diff
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING diff > 1000
)
  Result: 14

Result: 1 region had both male and female population increases with a growth rate difference > 0.5%.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT region) AS regions_with_growth FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_male,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_male,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS start_female,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_female
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING ((end_male - start_male) * 100.0 / start_male) - ((end_female - start_female) * 100.0 / start_female) > 0.5
)
  Result: 2
  Query: WITH male_growth AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END) AS start_male,

  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"

SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_growth
FROM (
  SELECT 
    m.region,
    m.start_male, m.end_male,
    f.start_female, f.end_female,
    ((m.end_male - m.start_male) * 100.0 / m.start_male) AS male_growth_rate,
    ((f.end_female - f.start_female) * 100.0 / f.start_female) AS female_growth_rate
  FROM male_growth m
  JOIN female_growth f ON m.region = f.region
  WHERE m.end_male > m.start_male AND f.end_female > f.start_female
) subquery
WHERE ABS(male_growth_rate - female_growth_rate) > 0.5;
  Result: 1

         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value END)) >

         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END))
)

Prompt: How many regions had a population change pattern opposite to the national trend?
Result: 3 regions had a population change pattern opposite to the national trend.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH NationalTrend AS (
  SELECT 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS national_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
),
RegionalTrends AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS regional_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_opposite_trend
FROM RegionalTrends, NationalTrend
WHERE (regional_change > 0 AND national_change < 0) OR (regional_change < 0 AND national_change > 0);
  Result: 3
  Query: WITH NationalTrend AS (
  SELECT 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
    SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS national_change
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'

RegionalTrends AS (

    "ČR, kraje" AS region,

  AND end_population."Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem'

Result: 11 regions had a higher percentage of women at period end despite a population decrease.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT "ČR, kraje") AS region_count FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS start_population,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value END) AS end_female_population,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING start_population > end_population AND (end_female_population * 100.0 / end_population) > 50
) AS filtered_regions;
  Result: 11
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT "ČR, kraje") AS region_count FROM (

  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"

Prompt: What is the correlation coefficient between initial population size and population change rate?
Result: The correlation coefficient between the initial population size and the population change rate is **1.5092957797836771e-06**.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH initial_population AS (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, value AS initial_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem'
    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
),
end_population AS (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, value AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem'
    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
)
SELECT 
  (SUM((initial_population - avg_initial) * (change_rate - avg_change_rate)) / 
   (SQRT(SUM((initial_population - avg_initial) * (initial_population - avg_initial))) * 
    SQRT(SUM((change_rate - avg_change_rate) * (change_rate - avg_change_rate))))) AS correlation_coefficient
FROM (
  SELECT 
    i.region,
    i.initial_population,
    (e.end_population - i.initial_population) * 1.0 / i.initial_population AS change_rate,
    AVG(i.initial_population) OVER () AS avg_initial,
    AVG((e.end_population - i.initial_population) * 1.0 / i.initial_population) OVER () AS avg_change_rate
  FROM initial_population i
  JOIN end_population e
  ON i.region = e.region
) subquery;
  Result: Error: Query error: no such function: SQRT
  Query: WITH initial_population AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, value AS initial_population FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' ), end_population AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, value AS end_population FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' ) SELECT (SUM((initial_population - avg_initial) * (change_rate - avg_change_rate)) / (POWER(SUM((initial_population - avg_initial) * (initial_population - avg_initial)), 0.5) * POWER(SUM((change_rate - avg_change_rate) * (change_rate - avg_change_rate)), 0.5))) AS correlation_coefficient FROM ( SELECT i.region, i.initial_population, (e.end_population - i.initial_population) * 1.0 / i.initial_population AS change_rate, AVG(i.initial_population) OVER () AS avg_initial, AVG((e.end_population - i.initial_population) * 1.0 / i.initial_population) OVER () AS avg_change_rate FROM initial_population i JOIN end_population e ON i.region = e.region ) subquery;

Prompt: What is the average demographic transition index for regions with more than 5% of national population?
Result: The average demographic transition index for regions with more than 5% of the national population is 0.9993338901594747.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH RegionalPopulation AS (
  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(value) AS total_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem'
    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),
NationalPopulation AS (
  SELECT 
    SUM(value) AS national_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem'
    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko'
),
FilteredRegions AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    total_population
  FROM RegionalPopulation, NationalPopulation
  WHERE total_population > 0.05 * national_population
)
SELECT 
  region,
  AVG(value) AS avg_demographic_transition_index
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Ukazatel" LIKE '%obyvatel na konci období%'
  AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
  AND "ČR, kraje" IN (SELECT region FROM FilteredRegions)
GROUP BY region
LIMIT 5;
  Result: Error: Query error: no such column: region
  Query: WITH RegionalPopulation AS ( SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, SUM(value) AS total_population FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' GROUP BY "ČR, kraje" ), NationalPopulation AS ( SELECT SUM(value) AS national_population FROM OBY01PDT01 WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' ), FilteredRegions AS ( SELECT region FROM RegionalPopulation, NationalPopulation WHERE total_population > 0.05 * national_population ) SELECT AVG(CAST(end_population.value AS FLOAT) / CAST(start_population.value AS FLOAT)) AS avg_demographic_transition_index FROM OBY01PDT01 AS start_population JOIN OBY01PDT01 AS end_population ON start_population."ČR, kraje" = end_population."ČR, kraje" AND start_population."Kumulace čtvrtletí" = end_population."Kumulace čtvrtletí" WHERE start_population."Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' AND end_population."Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' AND start_population."ČR, kraje" IN (SELECT region FROM FilteredRegions);
  Result: 0.9993338901594747

  SELECT 
    "ČR, kraje" AS region,
    SUM(value) AS total_population

  WHERE "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem'
    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'

    AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko'
),
FilteredRegions AS (
  SELECT 
    region,
    total_population
  FROM RegionalPopulation, NationalPopulation
  WHERE total_population > 0.05 * national_population
)
SELECT 
  region,
  AVG(value) AS avg_demographic_transition_index
FROM OBY01PDT01
WHERE "Ukazatel" LIKE '%obyvatel na konci období%'

    HAVING region != 'Česko' AND population_change > 0

Prompt: How many regions had both male and female population increases with growth rate difference > 0.5%?
Result: 1 region had both male and female population increases with a growth rate difference greater than 0.5%.
Queries and Results:
  Query: WITH male_growth AS (
    SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
           (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - muži' THEN value END) - 
            MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END)) * 100.0 / 
            MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - muži' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_male
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
),

female_growth AS (
    SELECT "ČR, kraje" AS region, 
           (MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - ženy' THEN value END) - 
            MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END)) * 100.0 / 
            MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - ženy' THEN value END) AS growth_rate_female
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024' AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)

SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_growth
FROM male_growth
JOIN female_growth ON male_growth.region = female_growth.region
WHERE ABS(male_growth.growth_rate_male - female_growth.growth_rate_female) > 0.5
  AND male_growth.growth_rate_male > 0
  AND female_growth.growth_rate_female > 0;
  Result: 1

SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_growth
FROM male_growth
JOIN female_growth ON male_growth.region = female_growth.region
WHERE ABS(male_growth.growth_rate_male - female_growth.growth_rate_female) > 0.5
  AND male_growth.growth_rate_male > 0
  AND female_growth.growth_rate_female > 0;
  Result: 1

Prompt: What is the total number of regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes exceeded 1000?
Result: The total number of regions where the absolute difference between male and female population changes exceeded 1000 is 14.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT "ČR, kraje") AS region_count
FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
             SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) AS diff
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING diff > 1000
)
  Result: 14
  Query: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT "ČR, kraje") AS region_count
FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%muži%' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
             SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" LIKE '%ženy%' THEN value ELSE 0 END)) AS diff
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING diff > 1000
)
  Result: 14

    SELECT 
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS national_change
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "ČR, kraje" = 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
),
RegionalTrends AS (
    SELECT 
        "ČR, kraje" AS region,
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) - 
        SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS regional_change
    FROM OBY01PDT01
    WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko' AND "Kumulace čtvrtletí" = 'Q1-Q3 2024'
    GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
)
SELECT COUNT(*) AS regions_with_opposite_trend
FROM RegionalTrends, NationalTrend
WHERE (regional_change > 0 AND national_change < 0) OR (regional_change < 0 AND national_change > 0);

         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS end_population,
         SUM(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Střední stav obyvatel - celkem' THEN value ELSE 0 END) AS mid_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
  HAVING end_population > mid_population
)
  Result: 7

  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE metric IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem')

Prompt: What is the average population rate of change for regions with more than 1 million residents?
Result: The average population rate of change for regions with more than 1 million residents is 0.0014294573090641652.
Queries and Results:
  Query: SELECT AVG((end_population.value - start_population.value) * 1.0 / start_population.value) AS avg_rate_of_change
FROM (
  SELECT region, 
         MAX(CASE WHEN metric = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS start_population,
         MAX(CASE WHEN metric = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE metric IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem')
    AND region != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY region
  HAVING MAX(CASE WHEN metric = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) > 1000000
) AS population_data;
  Result: Error: Query error: no such column: region
  Query: SELECT AVG((end_population - start_population) * 1.0 / start_population) AS avg_rate_of_change
FROM (
  SELECT "ČR, kraje", 
         MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem' THEN value END) AS start_population,
         MAX(CASE WHEN "Ukazatel" = 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem' THEN value END) AS end_population
  FROM OBY01PDT01
  WHERE "Ukazatel" IN ('Počet obyvatel na počátku období - celkem', 'Počet obyvatel na konci období - celkem')
    AND "ČR, kraje" != 'Česko'
  GROUP BY "ČR, kraje"
